<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a></i>.

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ketch.html>ketch</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:small.html>small</a> two-masted <a href = vnd.unilang:vessel.html>vessel</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:missing.html>missing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:please.html>Please</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:add.html>add</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:discuss.html>discuss</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
